\DoxyCodeLine{00470\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ 24\ byte\ string\ class\ (can\ be\ as\ small\ as\ 17\ for\ x64\ and\ 13\ for\ x86)\ that\ can\ hold\ strings\ with\ length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00471\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ up\ to\ 23\ chars\ on\ the\ stack\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ the\ last\ byte\ of\ the\ buffer\ is\ used\ for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00472\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ -\/\ the\ highest\ bit\ -\/\ if\ "{}0"{}\ then\ it\ is\ small\ -\/\ otherwise\ its\ "{}1"{}\ (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00473\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ capacity\ left\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ using\ the\ lowest\ 5\ bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00474\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ 2\ bits\ are\ left\ unused\ -\/\ the\ second\ and\ third\ highest\ ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00475\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ acts\ as\ a\ null\ terminator\ if\ strlen()\ is\ 23\ (24\ including\ the\ null\ terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00476\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ the\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ remains\ "{}0"{}\ ("{}as\ well\ as\ the\ capacity\ left"{})\ so\ its\ OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00477\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Idea\ taken\ from\ this\ lecture\ about\ the\ string\ implementation\ of\ facebook/folly\ -\/\ fbstring}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03217\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Each\ thread\ has\ a\ different\ atomic\ that\ it\ operates\ on.\ If\ more\ than\ NumLanes\ threads}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03222\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ minimal\ to\ no\ overhead\ in\ determining\ the\ correct\ atomic\ for\ the\ current\ thread.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03224\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 1.\ A\ global\ static\ counter\ laneCounter\ counts\ continuously\ up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03225\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 2.\ Each\ successive\ thread\ will\ use\ modulo\ operation\ of\ that\ counter\ so\ it\ gets\ an\ atomic}}
